<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Label</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Scrubber</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Control</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Input</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.IncrementTrigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.DecrementTrigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Control</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="min-and-max" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#min-and-max"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Min and Max</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Pass the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">min</code> prop or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">max</code> prop to set an upper and lower limit for the input. By default, the input will restrict the
value to stay within the specified range.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To allow values outside the min/max range, set <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">clampValueOnBlur</code> to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">false</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<h3 id="precision" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#precision"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Precision</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">In some cases, you might need the value to be rounded to specific decimal points. Set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">formatOptions</code> and provide
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Intl.NumberFormatOptions</code> such as <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">maximumFractionDigits</code> or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">minimumFractionDigits</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8phanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8phanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8phanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="scrubbing" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#scrubbing"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Scrubbing</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The NumberInput supports the scrubber interaction pattern. To use this pattern, render the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">NumberInput.Scrubber</code>
component. It uses the Pointer lock API and tracks the pointer movement. It also renders a virtual cursor which mimics
the real cursor&#x27;s pointer.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8vhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8vhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8vhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="mouse-wheel" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#mouse-wheel"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Mouse Wheel</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The NumberInput exposes a way to increment/decrement the value using the mouse wheel event. To activate this, set the
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">allowMouseWheel</code> prop to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">true</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_95hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_95hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_95hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="formatting" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#formatting"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Formatting</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To apply custom formatting to the input&#x27;s value, set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">formatOptions</code> and provide <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Intl.NumberFormatOptions</code> such as
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">style</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">currency</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="field" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#field"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Field</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field</code> component helps manage form-related state and accessibility attributes of a number input. It includes
handling ARIA labels, helper text, and error text to ensure proper accessibility.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the number input is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useNumberInput</code> hook.
This way you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="scrubber" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#scrubber"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Scrubber</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">NumberInput.Scrubber</code> component provides an interactive scrub area that allows users to drag to change the input
value. It renders as a <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">&lt;div&gt;</code> element and displays a custom cursor element during scrubbing interactions.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">This component utilizes the <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Pointer_Lock_API" class="link">Pointer Lock API</a> for
smooth dragging interactions.</p>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Note:</strong> Browsers may show a notification when the Pointer Lock API is activated. The scrubber is automatically
disabled in Safari to prevent layout shifts.</p>
</blockquote>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">When controlling the NumberInput component, it&#x27;s recommended to use string values instead of converting to numbers. This
is especially important when using <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">formatOptions</code> for currency or locale-specific formatting.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> [</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">value</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">setValue</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> useState</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;0&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Root</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> onValueChange</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">details</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> setValue</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(details.value)</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  {</span><span style="color:#8B949E">/* ... */</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Converting values to numbers can cause issues with locale-specific formatting, particularly for currencies that use
different decimal and thousands separators (e.g., <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">1.523,30</code> vs <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">1,523.30</code>). By keeping values as strings, you preserve
the correct formatting and avoid parsing issues.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">If you need to submit a numeric value in your form, use a hidden input that reads <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">valueAsNumber</code> from
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">NumberInput.Context</code>:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Root</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> onValueChange</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">details</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> setValue</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(details.value)</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Input</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Context</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">    {</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">context</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">input</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> type</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;hidden&quot;</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> name</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;amount&quot;</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">context.valueAsNumber</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Context</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">NumberInput.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>

<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Complies with the <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/spinbutton/" class="link">Spinbutton WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>

By default, the input will restrict the\nvalue to stay within the specified range.\n\n**Example: min-max**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/react/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const MinMax = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root className={styles.Root} min={0} max={10}\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger className={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger className={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n\u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n\u003e To allow values outside the min/max range, set `clampValueOnBlur` to `false`.\n\n### Precision\n\nIn some cases, you might need the value to be rounded to specific decimal points. Set the `formatOptions` and provide\n`Intl.NumberFormatOptions` such as `maximumFractionDigits` or `minimumFractionDigits`.\n\n**Example: fraction-digits**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/react/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const FractionDigits = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root\n    className={styles.Root}\n    formatOptions={{ minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 3 }}\n    defaultValue=\"1.00\"\n  \u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger className={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger className={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const FractionDigits = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root\n    class={styles.Root}\n    formatOptions={{ minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 3 }}\n    defaultValue=\"1.00\"\n  \u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger class={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger class={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root\n    :class=\"styles.Root\"\n    :formatOptions=\"{ minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 3 }\"\n    defaultValue=\"1.00\"\n  \u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.TriggerGroup\"\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger :class=\"styles.IncrementTrigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger :class=\"styles.DecrementTrigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/svelte/number-input'\n  import { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cNumberInput.Root\n  class={styles.Root}\n  formatOptions={{ minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 3 }}\n  defaultValue=\"1.00\"\n\u003e\n  \u003cNumberInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n  \u003cNumberInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger class={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n        \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger class={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n        \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n\u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Scrubbing\n\nThe NumberInput supports the scrubber interaction pattern. To use this pattern, render the `NumberInput.Scrubber`\ncomponent. It uses the Pointer lock API and tracks the pointer movement. It also renders a virtual cursor which mimics\nthe real cursor's pointer.\n\n**Example: scrubber**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/react/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon, ArrowLeftRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const Scrubber = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"32\"\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Scrubber className={styles.Scrubber}\u003e\n        \u003cArrowLeftRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.Scrubber\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input className={styles.Input} data-has-scrubber /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger className={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger className={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/number-input'\nimport { ArrowLeftRightIcon, ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const Scrubber = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"32\"\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Scrubber class={styles.Scrubber}\u003e\n        \u003cArrowLeftRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.Scrubber\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input class={styles.Input} data-has-scrubber /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger class={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger class={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/number-input'\nimport { ArrowLeftRightIcon, ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" defaultValue=\"32\"\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label    \u003cArrowLeftRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.Scrubber\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" data-has-scrubber /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.TriggerGroup\"\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger :class=\"styles.IncrementTrigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger :class=\"styles.DecrementTrigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/svelte/number-input'\n  import { ArrowLeftRightIcon, ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n    \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger class={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n        \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger class={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n        \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n\u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Mouse Wheel\n\nThe NumberInput exposes a way to increment/decrement the value using the mouse wheel event. To activate this, set the\n`allowMouseWheel` prop to `true`.\n\n**Example: mouse-wheel**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/react/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const MouseWheel = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root className={styles.Root} allowMouseWheel\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger className={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger className={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const MouseWheel = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root class={styles.Root} allowMouseWheel\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger class={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger class={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n :class=\"styles.Root\" allowMouseWheel\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.TriggerGroup\"\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n\u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Formatting\n\nTo apply custom formatting to the input's value, set the `formatOptions` and provide `Intl.NumberFormatOptions` such as\n`style` and `currency`.\n\n**Example: formatting**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/react/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const Formatting = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root\n    className={styles.Root}\n    formatOptions={{\n      style: 'currency',\n      currency: 'USD',\n    }}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger className={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger className={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const Formatting = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root\n    class={styles.Root}\n    formatOptions={{\n      style: 'currency',\n      currency: 'USD',\n    }}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger class={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger class={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :formatOptions=\"{ style: 'currency', currency: 'USD' }\"\u003e\n Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/svelte/number-input'\n  import { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n\u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Field\n\nThe `Field` component helps manage form-related state and accessibility attributes of a number input. It includes\nhandling ARIA labels, helper text, and error text to ensure proper accessibility.\n\n**Example: with-field**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/react/field'\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/react/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root className={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cdiv className={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n          \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger className={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger className={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText className={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText className={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/solid/field'\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n          \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger class={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger class={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText class={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText class={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/vue/field'\nimport { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cField.Root :class=\"field.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n        \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.TriggerGroup\"\u003e\n          \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger :class=\"styles.IncrementTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger :class=\"styles.DecrementTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText :class=\"field.HelperText\"\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText :class=\"field.ErrorText\"\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Field } from '@ark-ui/svelte/field'\n  import { NumberInput } from '@ark-ui/svelte/number-input'\n  import { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import field from 'styles/field.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cNumberInput.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger class={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n  \u003cField.HelperText class={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n  \u003cField.ErrorText class={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n\u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the number input is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useNumberInput` hook.\nThis way you can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { NumberInput, useNumberInput } from '@ark-ui/react/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const numberInput = useNumberInput()\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003evalueAsNumber: {numberInput.valueAsNumber}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={numberInput}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cNumberInput.Input className={styles.Input} /\u003e\n          \u003cdiv className={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n            \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger className={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger className={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { NumberInput, useNumberInput } from '@ark-ui/solid/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const numberInput = useNumberInput()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003evalueAsNumber: {numberInput().valueAsNumber}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={numberInput}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cNumberInput.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n            \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger class={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger class={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { NumberInput, useNumberInput } from '@ark-ui/vue/number-input'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\nconst numberInput = useNumberInput()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003coutput\u003evalueAsNumber: {{ numberInput.valueAsNumber }}\u003c/output\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"numberInput\"\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.Input :class=\"styles.Input\" /\u003e\n        \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.TriggerGroup\"\u003e\n          \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger :class=\"styles.IncrementTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger :class=\"styles.DecrementTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { NumberInput, useNumberInput } from '@ark-ui/svelte/number-input'\n  import { ChevronDownIcon, ChevronUpIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/number-input.module.css'\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const numberInput = useNumberInput({ id })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003coutput\u003evalueAsNumber: {numberInput().valueAsNumber}\u003c/output\u003e\n  \u003cNumberInput.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={numberInput}\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/NumberInput.Label\u003e\n    \u003cNumberInput.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cNumberInput.Input class={styles.Input} /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.TriggerGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.IncrementTrigger class={styles.IncrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronUpIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.IncrementTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cNumberInput.DecrementTrigger class={styles.DecrementTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/NumberInput.DecrementTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/NumberInput.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/NumberInput.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n## Guides\n\n### Scrubber\n\nThe `NumberInput.Scrubber` component provides an interactive scrub area that allows users to drag to change the input\nvalue. It renders as a `\u003cdiv\u003e` element and displays a custom cursor element during scrubbing interactions.\n\nThis component utilizes the [Pointer Lock API](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Pointer_Lock_API) for\nsmooth dragging interactions.\n\n\u003e **Note:** Browsers may show a notification when the Pointer Lock API is activated. The scrubber is automatically\n\u003e disabled in Safari to prevent layout shifts.\n\n### Controlled\n\nWhen controlling the NumberInput component, it's recommended to use string values instead of converting to numbers. This\nis especially important when using `formatOptions` for currency or locale-specific formatting.\n\n```tsx\nconst [value, setValue] = useState('0')\n\n\u003cNumberInput.Root value={value} onValueChange={(details) =\u003e setValue(details.value)}\u003e\n  {/* ... */}\n\u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n```\n\nConverting values to numbers can cause issues with locale-specific formatting, particularly for currencies that use\ndifferent decimal and thousands separators (e.g., `1.523,30` vs `1,523.30`). By keeping values as strings, you preserve\nthe correct formatting and avoid parsing issues.\n\nIf you need to submit a numeric value in your form, use a hidden input that reads `valueAsNumber` from\n`NumberInput.Context`:\n\n```tsx\n\u003cNumberInput.Root value={value} onValueChange={(details) =\u003e setValue(details.value)}\u003e\n  \u003cNumberInput.Input /\u003e\n  \u003cNumberInput.Context\u003e\n    {(context) =\u003e \u003cinput type=\"hidden\" name=\"amount\" value={context.valueAsNumber} /\u003e}\n  \u003c/NumberInput.Context\u003e\n\u003c/NumberInput.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Props\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `allowMouseWheel` | `boolean` | No | Whether to allow mouse wheel to change the value |\n| `allowOverflow` | `boolean` | No | Whether to allow the value overflow the min/max range |\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `clampValueOnBlur` | `boolean` | No | Whether to clamp the value when the input loses focus (blur) |\n| `defaultValue` | `string` | No | The initial value of the input when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the value of the input. |\n| `disabled` | `boolean` | No | Whether the number input is disabled. |\n| `focusInputOnChange` | `boolean` | No | Whether to focus input when the value changes |\n| `form` | `string` | No | The associate form of the input element. |\n| `formatOptions` | `NumberFormatOptions` | No | The options to pass to the `Intl.NumberFormat` constructor |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique identifier of the machine. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{\n  root: string\n  label: string\n  input: string\n  incrementTrigger: string\n  decrementTrigger: string\n  scrubber: string\n}\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the number input. Useful for composition. |\n| `inputMode` | `InputMode` | No | Hints at the type of data that might be entered by the user. It also determines\nthe type of keyboard shown to the user on mobile devices |\n| `invalid` | `boolean` | No | Whether the number input value is invalid. |\n| `locale` | `string` | No | The current locale. Based on the BCP 47 definition. |\n| `max` | `number` | No | The maximum value of the number input |\n| `min` | `number` | No | The minimum value of the number input |\n| `name` | `string` | No | The name attribute of the number input. Useful for form submission. |\n| `onFocusChange` | `(details: FocusChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function invoked when the number input is focused |\n| `onValueChange` | `(details: ValueChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function invoked when the value changes |\n| `onValueCommit` | `(details: ValueChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function invoked when the value is committed (when the input is blurred or the Enter key is pressed) |\n| `onValueInvalid` | `(details: ValueInvalidDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function invoked when the value overflows or underflows the min/max range |\n| `pattern` | `string` | No | The pattern used to check the \u003cinput\u003e element's value against |\n| `readOnly` | `boolean` | No | Whether the number input is readonly |\n| `required` | `boolean` | No | Whether the number input is required |\n| `spinOnPress` | `boolean` | No | Whether to spin the value when the increment/decrement button is pressed |\n| `step` | `number` | No | The amount to increment or decrement the value by |\n| `translations` | `IntlTranslations` | No | Specifies the localized strings that identifies the accessibility elements and their states |\n| `value` | `string` | No | The controlled value of the input |\n\n\n**Root Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | number-input |\n| `[data-part]` | root |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-focus]` | Present when focused |\n| `[data-invalid]` | Present when invalid |\n| `[data-scrubbing]` |  |\n\n\n**Control Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Control Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | number-input |\n| `[data-part]` | control |\n| `[data-focus]` | Present when focused |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-invalid]` | Present when invalid |\n| `[data-scrubbing]` |  |\n\n\n**DecrementTrigger Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**DecrementTrigger Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | number-input |\n| `[data-part]` | decrement-trigger |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-scrubbing]` |  |\n\n\n**IncrementTrigger Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**IncrementTrigger Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | number-input |\n| `[data-part]` | increment-trigger |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-scrubbing]` |  |\n\n\n**Input Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Input Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | number-input |\n| `[data-part]` | input |\n| `[data-invalid]` | Present when invalid |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-scrubbing]` |  |\n\n\n**Label Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Label Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value Present when invalid |\n| `[data-required]` | Present when required |\n| `[data-scrubbing]` |  |\n\n\n**RootProvider Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description
